  <p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.247584s;">Last updated 28/06/23</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.249814s;" class="preSlide">COOKIES NOTICE</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.252045s;">Emergent Entertainment websites (collectively “Emergent Entertainment” in this document) refer to sites hosted by Emergent Entertainment. This includes domains owned by Emergent Entertainment, such as product websites, other related domains and subdomains thereof. This cookie policy describes how Emergent Entertainment collects and uses cookies.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.254275s;"> We use cookies, pixels and tags (which we shall collectively define as “Cookies”) for a variety of purposes which are described in this Cookie Policy. By accepting our cookie banner you consent to the storing and accessing of Cookies on your device in accordance with the terms of this Cookie Policy.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.256506s;" class="preSlide">WHAT ARE COOKIES AND WHAT DO THEY DO?</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.258736s;">A cookie is a very small text document, which often includes an anonymous unique identifier. When you visit the Emergent Entertainment website, a computer asks your computer for permission to store this file in a part of your hard drive specifically designated for cookies.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.260967s;"> For further details on cookies, please visit the website All About Cookies where you can find comprehensive information on Cookies.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.263197s;" class="preSlide">CONSENT AND BLOCKING OF THE USE OF COOKIES ON THE EMERGENT ENTERTAINMENT WEBSITE</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.265428s;">By navigating away from the home page of the Emergent Entertainment web site and continuing to use the Emergent Entertainment website, you are consenting to our use of the Cookies described in this Cookie Policy.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.267658s;"> If you do not consent to Emergent Entertainment using Cookies or, having previously consented to our use of Cookies, you decide to block such use then please read the next section of this Cookie Policy entitled “Blocking our Use of Cookies”.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.269888s;" class="preSlide">Blocking our Use of Cookies</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.272119s;"> You can block our use of Cookies at any time by activating the settings in your web browser. Please visit All About Cookies where you can find comprehensive information on cookie management for a wide variety of web browsers.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.274349s;" class="preSlide">What Happens if I Block Cookies?</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.27658s;">If you choose to withhold consent to Emergent Entertainment's use of Cookies, or subsequently block Cookies that you previously consented to, some aspects of the Emergent Entertainment web site may not work properly and you may not be able to access all or part of our Emergent Entertainment website.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.27881s;" class="preSlide">HOW WE USE COOKIES ON THE EMERGENT Entertainment WEBSITE</h3><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.281041s;" class="preSlide">Session Cookies</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.283271s;">We use Cookies to allow the Emergent Entertainment web site to uniquely identify a user's browsing session on the Emergent Entertainment web site and to allow us to coordinate this information with data from our Emergent Entertainment web site server.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.285502s;" class="preSlide">Analytics </h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.287732s;">We use Google's “analytics” Cookies which, in conjunction with our web server's log files, allow us to identify unique, but anonymous users. These Cookies can also calculate the aggregate number of people visiting our Emergent Entertainment website, the date and time of a user's visit to the Emergent Entertainment website, the pages a user has viewed and the time spent by users at the Emergent Entertainment website. This helps us gather feedback so that we can improve the Emergent Entertainment web site and better serve our users. Further information on each Cookie is set out in the list below.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.289963s;" class="preSlide">Cross platform advertising and user recognition</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.292193s;">We also use Cookies provided by Facebook and Twitter. These Cookies operate in different ways but they are both used in connection with Emergent Entertainment advertising served to a user of the Emergent Entertainment website on Twitter and Facebook, the recognition of such users and the devices used by the user to access Twitter, Facebook and the Emergent Entertainment web site.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.294424s;">Further information on each Cookie is set out in the table below.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.296654s;" class="preSlide">THIRD PARTY WEB SITES AND PLATFORMS</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.298885s;">Your use of third party web sites and platforms such as Twitter, LinkedIn and Facebook, and the privacy practices of these platforms, are governed by separate terms, conditions and policies for which Emergent Entertainment is not responsible. You should review Twitter’s and Facebook’s terms, conditions and policies where you will find more details on how information about you is used on their platforms and how you can set your privacy preferences. You can find more information about the individual Cookies we use and the purposes for which they are used in the list below:</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.301115s;" class="preSlide">Google Analytics</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.303346s;">_ga</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.305576s;">This Cookie is placed by Google. It enables Emergent Entertainment to learn information about our users' use of the Emergent Entertainment website such as the time of visit, the pages viewed, whether the user has visited before and the web site visited prior to visiting the Emergent Entertainment website.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.307807s;">To opt-out please see https://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptout</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.310037s;" class="preSlide">Twitter Conversion Tracker</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.312268s;">uwt.js </p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.314498s;">This Cookie is placed by Twitter. It enables Emergent Entertainment to learn how our users have interacted with Emergent Entertainment advertising served to them on Twitter. It also enables Emergent Entertainment to identify users who have used their mobile device to view Emergent Entertainment advertising on Twitter and later came to the Emergent Entertainment website on a desktop computer.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.316729s;">To opt-out please see http://optout.aboutads.info/#/</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.318959s;" class="preSlide">Facebook Pixel</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.32119s;">fbevents.js </p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.32342s;">This Cookie is placed by Facebook. It enables Emergent Entertainment to measure, optimise and build audiences for advertising campaigns served on Facebook. In particular it enables Emergent Entertainment to see how our users move between devices when accessing the Emergent Entertainment website and Facebook, to ensure that Emergent Entertainment’s Facebook advertising is seen by our users most likely to be interested in such advertising by analysing which content a user has viewed and interacted with on the Emergent Entertainment website.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.325651s;">To opt-out please see https://www.facebook.com/ads/preferences</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.327881s;" class="preSlide">Cookie Pop Up</h3><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.330112s;">cookieAccept  </p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.332342s;">This Cookie is placed by Emergent Entertainment. It is used to record when a user of the Emergent Entertainment web site has viewed the Cookie notice to prevent it re-appearing on return visits. Most of our cookies expire within 30 days, although our analytics cookies may persist for 1 year.</p>
</div>



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>

Your Rights In Relation To Your Personal Data You have certain rights over the way we process personal data relating to you. We aim to comply without undue delay, and within one month at the latest, in response to any requests submitted by you to us: for a copy of personal data we are processing about you and/or to have inaccuracies corrected; to restrict, stop processing, or to delete your personal data; for a machine-readable copy of your personal data, which you can use with another service provider. Where it is technically feasible, you can ask us to send this information directly to another provider if you prefer; and to make a complaint to a data protection regulator. You may contact them at: <a href="https://ico.org.uk/concerns/">https://ico.org.uk/concerns/</a>. To make a request in relation to any of the aforementioned rights, please send your request to info@resurgence-game.io. You may request deletion of your personal data by sending an e-mail to <a href="mailto:info@maze-theory.com">info@maze-theory.com</a>. Please note that some information may remain in our private records after deletion. We may use any aggregated data derived from or incorporating your personal data but not in any manner that would identify you personally For data processing activities for which we rely upon your consent, you can withdraw your consent at any time by using the tools provided (if applicable, such as in-Game or through your device settings) or otherwise by contacting us at <a href="mailto:info@maze-theory.com">info@maze-theory.com</a></p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.443866s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.446097s;">2. Disclosure of your personal data</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.448327s;">We will share your personal data with third parties only in the ways that are described in this Policy. Group, suppliers, subcontractors, service providers. We keep your personal data confidential, but may disclose it to any member of our corporate group, our personnel, suppliers or subcontractors insofar as it is reasonably necessary for the purposes set out in this Policy. Government authorities. In addition, we may disclose your personal data to the extent that we are required to do so by law (which may include to government bodies and law enforcement agencies); in connection with any legal proceedings or prospective legal proceedings; and to establish, exercise or defend our legal rights (including providing information to others for the purposes of fraud prevention). Potential acquirers or investors. If we are involved in a merger, acquisition, or sale of all or a portion of our business or assets, the personal data we hold may be included as part of that sale, in which case you will be notified via email, your account and/or a prominent notice on the website of any changes in ownership or use of your personal data, as well as any choices you may have. Enforcement. We may also disclose your personal information to third parties in order to enforce or apply the terms of agreements, to investigate potential breaches, or to protect the rights, property or safety of us, our personnel or customers, or others. Stores. We may also disclose your personal data, to the extent necessary, to game / application stores or platforms (such as the Apple App Store and Google Play Store) if that is required, for example, for fulfilment of an order you make (e.g. if needed to fulfil a mobile game DLC order) or in order to investigate or prevent fraud. Such platforms and stores may also process your information in order to provide you with cross-device access to your current position in the Game and your in-Game progression, for example. We only permit our suppliers and subcontractors to process your personal data for specified purposes and in accordance with our instructions. All our third-party service providers are required to take appropriate security measures to protect your personal data.<br><br>We will only hold data about you for as long as necessary, bearing in mind the purpose for which that data was collected, or as otherwise described in this Policy. To determine the appropriate retention period for personal data, we consider the amount, nature, and sensitivity of the personal data, the potential risk of harm from unauthorised use or disclosure of your personal data, the purposes for which we process your personal data and whether we can achieve those purposes through other means, and the applicable legal requirements.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.450558s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.452788s;">3. The below explains the main cookies we use in our Websites and Games and why:</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.488476s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.490706s;"><strong>Google Analytics (on our Websites) _ga</strong></p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.492937s;">This Google cookie is placed on our Websites.
